<Time>1405569736039</Time><rating>5< /rating><review>I took my girlfriend here for dinner and we both loved it!

Food: The food was delicious! We ordered a few items.

Edamame (Garlic Spicy) - It was very delicious! The roasted garlic was nice and crispy. The Japanese chilis were just spicy enough without making the dish overpowering. One order of this was just not enough!
Crazy Eel (9pc Roll)- Spicy tuna, avocado, cream cheese topped with BBQ eel, spicy eel sauce. THIS ROLL WAS THE BOMB! The BBQ eel was so tender that it melts in your mouth! This totally had the umami factor to it :) My girlfriend and I could have easily eaten one roll each.
K-1 (9pc Roll) - Spicy tuna, avocado, cilantro topped with albacore, special ponzu sauce. The roll was good. However, I would have preferred it without the cilantro. I really really dislike cilantro. LOL!
Lollipop (6 pc Roll) - Tuna, salmon, yellowtail, albacore, avocado wrapped with cucumber creamy & hot sauce. This was a very refreshing roll to eat. The fish was fresh. The cucumber was the refreshing part of the roll. The roll was on a toothpick henceforth it was called the lollipop roll.

Service: The waitress was attentive and nice. We were seated quickly when we arrived. The sushi chef even came around to greet us and make sure everything was satisfactory.

Overall, the place was clean and the service was outstanding. The food was AMAZING!<//review><pictures>None< /pictures>< resp>

<username>Filipe Nabarrete< /username><Date>1542914053082<//Date><rating>3</rating><review>(Translated by Google) The park leaves a lot to be desired in various aspects, first the service compared to Orlando is 5 out of 10 it leaves a lot to be desired and ends the magic and experience of the visitor, then it has many closed toys for renovation. Still, if you purchase the maxpass, you can get to know the park faster and enjoy the attractions more. As for the closing show, total frustration, the employees close some routes so that you cannot stop to take pictures during the show, to get a reasonable place that can see the fireworks, you need to arrive at least 40 minutes in advance. I would not go back to this park. It is not prepared for tourists it is more of a local park. It doesn't have the Disney magic you see in Orlando!

I feel that Dr. Jones listened to my issues and took into account my lifestyle, and it‚Äôs stresses on my body, as well as my concerns and desire to keep my back as healthy as possible, and addressed that thoroughly.

The office staff was great and the office was very clean.

I would definitely recommend them!<//text>

<UserId.>115404550884779971191</UserId.>< Text>
We had to travel to Deforest on business, our business completed it was lunch time.
Where to eat ? We were driving east on Cty. V and the parking lot at DeForest Family Restaurant was full. So we made a quick turn around and stopped. We found a place to park and went inside. Even though they were very busy we were seated right away. Our smiling waitress was right their with our drinks and gave us some time to look over the menu. They have a GREAT selection plus Sr. specials every day. We both chose the pork ribs, potatoes, peas, soup. In no time our meals were their and they were delicious. Both meals were very generous and we were both full when we were finished. The waitress returned several times to make sure all was well with our meals.
Convenient parking, lots of seating, friendly staff, quick service, delicious food and plenty of time to relax after our meal. All these will bring us back again.</Text>
